by O
Chicago O
architect O
Stephen O
Katz O
in O
2013, O

Eliza O
blends O
a O
beautiful O
technically O
derived O
form O
with O
superior O

and O
movement. O
The O
unique O
blade O
shape O
is O
designed O
to O
maximize O
air O
movement O
at O
the O
outer O
edge O
of O
the O
blade. O
The O
result O
is O
more O
efficient O
air O
velocity O
rings, O
less O

and O
greater O
motor O
optimization. O
Equally O

is O

Eliza O
fan’s O

visual O
statement O
which O
combines O
modern O
utility O
with O
minimalist O
geometry. O
Dimensions O
56" O
D O
Additional O
Details•Energy O
efficient, O
ultra-quiet, O

and O

DC O
motor O

Chair I-PRODUCT

Keep O
conversations O

by O
placing O
a O
pair O
of O
these O

a O

and O

when O
two O

Plush O

or O

for O
cushions). O

x O

Shipping O
& O
Returns O
How O
long O
does O
shipping O
and O
delivery O
take? O
In O
the O
Portland O
metro O
area, O
our O
lead O
time O
is O
12 O
to O
14 O
weeks. O
For O
the O
rest O
of O
the O
continental O
United O
States, O
lead O
times O
will O
include O
2 O
to O
4 O
additional O
weeks O
for O
shipping. O
Due O
to O
current O
supply O
chain O
challenges, O
please O
note O
that O
the O
lead O
time(s) O
provided O
at O
the O
time O
of O
sale O
are O
a O
representation O
of O
our O
understanding, O
in O
the O
moment, O
of O
the O
furniture O
or O
component O
part’s O
future O
availability. O
Lead O
times O
are O
subject O
to O
change O
and O
are O
influenced O
by O
many O
factors O
outside O
of O
our O
control. O
We O
will O
keep O
you O
advised O
of O
any O
delays O
that O
arise O
as O
the O
information O
is O
received. O
Can O
I O
pick O
my O
furniture O
up? O
We O
offer O
Will O
Call O
services O
for O
furniture O
delivered O
to O
Portland. O
A O
$125 O
fee O
applies, O
and O
furniture O
that O
is O
picked O
up O
by O
you O
(or O
your O
representative) O
from O
our O
delivery O
service O
warehouse O
must O
be O
inspected O
at O
the O
warehouse O
and O
signed O
off O
on O
as O
"in O
good O
condition" O
before O
it O
will O
be O
released O
to O
you. O
Perch O
cannot O
accept O
responsibility O
for O
any O
damage O
that O
occurs O
once O
the O
furniture O
is O
released. O
What O
if O
my O
furniture O
doesn't O
fit? O
The O
customer O
is O
responsible O
for O
verifying O
building O
access O
and O
all O
entry O
measurements O
(doorways, O
stairwells, O
elevators, O
etc.). O
Additional O
delivery O
charges O
may O
be O
assessed O
for O
walkups O
or O
extra O
time O
spent O
if O
the O
furniture O
does O
not O
fit O
via O
normal O
means. O
Furniture O
that O
does O
not O
fit O
will O
be O
refunded O
in O
store O
credit O
only O
and O
original O
shipping O
fees O
will O
not O
be O
credited. O
Additional O
shipping O
and O
delivery O
charges O
will O
apply O
to O
orders O
that O
use O
store O
credit. O

General O
Cleaning: O

plastic. O
Use O
a O

cleaner; O

cleaner; O
or O
a O

of O

water. O
Apply O

surface O
or O

and O

gently. O
The O
plastic O
injection O
moulding O
process O
produces O
large O
numbers O
of O
parts O
of O
high O
quality O
with O

Plastic O

form O
of O

to O

a O

The O

that O

is O

Description O
The O
Yves B-PRODUCT
desk I-PRODUCT
is O
an O
elegant O
and O
compact O
writing O
desk, O
with O
softly O
sculpted O
legs O
and O
a O
tiered O
top. O
It O
has O
an O
inlaid O
dark O
brown O
leather O
writing O
surface, O
two O
drawers O
and O
a O
cable O
access O
hole O
to O
each O
side O
at O
the O
rear O
of O
the O
desk. O
Please O
select O
the O
timber O
from O
the O
drop-downs O
to O
update O
the O
price. O
This O
item O
requires O
basic O
assembly O
or O
can O
be O
delivered O
white O
glove O
including O
assembly. O

Materials O

Black O
American O
walnut O
Black O
walnut O
is O
a O
hardwood O
with O
a O
rich O
and O
straight-grained O
timber, O
it O
can O
display O
many O
unique O
characteristics, O
such O
as O
knots O
and O
variations O
in O
depth O
of O
tone. O
The O
walnut O
we O
source O
is O
native O
to O
North O
America. O
We O
use O
a O
protective O
lacquer O
finish O
which O
enables O
the O
timber O
to O
age O
gracefully O
without O
heavy O
discolouration O
and O
withstand O
daily O
spillage. O
European O
oak O
European O
oak O
is O
a O
temperate O
white O
oak O
hardwood O
native O
to O
Europe. O
It O
presents O
a O
golden O
to O
light O
brown O
hue O
with O
a O
minimal O
grain O
pattern. O
We O
use O
a O
protective O
white O
oil O
finish O
to O
allow O
the O
timber O
to O
age O
gracefully O
without O
heavy O
discolouration O
and O
withstand O
daily O
spillage. O
Dark O
brown O
house O
leather O
Our O
house O
leather O
is O
a O
dark O
brown O
aniline O
leather. O
As O
such, O
it O
may O
reveal O
natural O
markings O
such O
as O
scarring, O
growth O
marks O
and O
variation O
in O
tone O
and O
colour. O
These O
markings O
are O
a O
part O
of O
the O
beauty O
of O
the O
leather O
which O
has O
been O
selected O
for O
its O
natural O

high O
quality O
and O
comfort. O
As O
a O
natural O
material O
it O
will O
age O
according O
to O
its O
environment, O
creating O
a O
beautiful O
patina O
over O
time. O
Care O
guide O
Oiled O
wood O
An O
oiled O
finish O
is O
a O
durable O
natural O
looking O
finish O
that O
can O
be O
revitalised O
(and O
if O
necessary, O
more O
easily O
repaired). O
Oiled O
finishes O
require O
some O
low O
level O
maintenance O
to O
keep O
the O
wood O
protected O
and O
looking O
its O
best. O
Day O
to O
day O
cleaning: O
• O
Wipe O
clean O
with O
a O
damp O
non-abrasive O
cloth, O
then O
using O
a O
dry O
cloth O
remove O
any O
excess O
moisture. O
• O
Wipe O
up O
wine, O
oil O
and O
any O
liquids O
that O
might O
stain O
as O
quickly O
as O
possible. O
• O
To O
ensure O
the O
finish O
remains O
as O
resilient O
as O
possible O
to O
staining O
we O
recommend O
Osmo O
Wash O
& O
Care O
(8016) O
as O
it O
contains O
soaps O
and O
oils O
to O
both O
nourish O
and O
prevent O
the O
wood O
from O
drying O
out. O
6 O
monthly O
replenishment O
/ O
more O
stubborn O
stains: O
• O
As O
the O
table O
is O
used O
it O
can O
dry O
out O
as O
the O
oil O
can O
thin O
with O
wear O
and O
washing O
with O
water O
alone. O
If O
the O
table O
looks O
dry O
or O
you O
have O
a O
more O
stubborn O
stain O
we O
recommend O
using O
a O

Osmo O
Liquid O
Wax O
Cleaner O
(white O
3087) O
for O
oak O
pieces O
and O
(clear O
3029) O
for O
walnut O
pieces O
Do O
not: O
• O
Leave O
any O
water, O
wine, O
oil O
or O
liquids O
that O
might O
stain O
– O
wipe O
up O
as O
quickly O
as O
possible. O
(Oil O
provides O
a O

finish, O
which O
means O

can O
penetrate O

surface O
if O

• O
Use O
ANY O
chemical O

products O
or O
bleach O
as O
this O
will O
remove O
the O
protective O
layer O
of O
oil O
and O

will O
then O
stain. O
Lacquered O
wood O
A O

finish O
requires O
very O

and O
resistant O

• O

clean O
with O

cloth O

buff O
off O
with O

cloth. O
Do O
not: O
• O
Leave O
any O
wine, O
oil O
or O
liquids O
that O
might O
stain O
– O
wipe O
up O
as O
quickly O
as O

• O
Use O
any O
abrasive O
cleaning O
products O
or O
bleach O
as O
this O
could O

the O
protective O
layer O
of O

House O
leather O
Our O
house O
leather O
is O
a O
pure O
aniline O
leather. O
As O

may O
reveal O
natural O
markings O

marks O
and O

in O

These O

a O

of O
the O
beauty O
of O
the O
leather O
which O
has O
been O
selected O
for O
its O
natural O
materiality, O
high O
quality O
and O
comfort. O
As O
a O
natural O
material O
it O
will O
age O
according O
to O
its O
environment, O
creating O
a O
beautiful O
patina O
over O
time. O
We O

furniture O

next O

Care O

Oiled O
wood O

• O

• O

• O

and O

Key O
Features O
- O
Mango O
Timber O
The O
timber O
used O
in O
this O
piece O
is O
sustainably O
sourced O
Mango O
Wood. O
Each O
plank O
is O
individually O
treated O
in O
a O
computer O
controlled O
kiln O
to O
reduce O
the O
chance O
of O
any O
cracks O
or O
warping O
in O
its O
long O
future O
as O
a O
furniture O
component. O
This O
piece O
has O
been O
handcrafted O
by O
one O
of O
our O
Vast O
Masters, O
these O
individual O
cabinet O
makers O
have O
been O
manufacturing O
Vast O
products O
for O
over O
a O
decade. O
Using O
traditional O
joinery O
techniques O
to O
maximise O
the O
timber's O
natural O
beauty O
is O
a O
big O
part O
of O
the O
unique O
look O
of O
each O
Vast O
product. O
We O
call O
this O
"working O
with O
the O
grain". O
After O
the O
joinery O
is O
complete O
it O
is O
then O
hand O
sanded O
and O
hand O
polished O
with O

of O
high O
grade O
German O
lacquer O
so O

last O
for O

Country O
of O

India O
Product O
Care O
- O
Timber O
Hardwood O
is O
a O
natural O
material O
which O
reacts O
to O
its O
environment O
and O
although O
our O
manufacturing O
process O
allows O
for O
normal O
expansion O
and O
contraction, O
extreme O
high O
or O
low O
humidity O
may O
cause O
more O
swelling O
than O
normal. O
To O
minimise O
movement O
and O
ensure O
longevity O
of O
your O
purchase O
we O
recommend O
taking O
good O
care O
of O
your O
piece O
as O
outlined O
below: O
Dust O
regularly O
with O
a O
clean O
cotton O
cloth; O
Use O
tablecloths, O
table O
runners O
and O
coasters O
to O
help O
prevent O
scratches O
to O
the O
surface O
and O
wipe O
up O
any O
spills O
immediately; O
To O
nourish O
and O
protect O
your O
furniture O
we O
recommend O
waxing O
with O
a O
natural O
beeswax O
every O
6-12 O
months. O
Only O
use O
natural O
wax, O
oil O
or O
water O
based O
cleaning O
products. O
Do O
not O
use O
solvent O
based O
cleaning O
products O
that O
may O
contain O
silicone O
or O
alcohol, O
as O
this O
may O
react O
and O
permanently O
damage O
the O
lacquer. O
Do O
not O
expose O
to O
fragrant O
oils, O
insect O
repellent O
lotion, O
or O
nail O
polish O
remover O
as O
these O
are O
often O
solvent O
based O
and O
will O
damage O
the O
lacquer O
Avoid O
placing O
your O
furniture O
near O
fireplaces, O
in O
direct O
sunlight O
or O
under O
heating/cooling O
vents. O
Do O
not O
leave O
hot O
items O
or O
ice O
cold O
items O
directly O
on O
the O
surface O
of O
the O
table O
as O
water O
marking O
may O
occur. O
Any O
metal O
work O
featuring O
on O
your O
product O
has O
been O
powder O
coated. O
Any O
damage O
to O
the O
surface O
should O

contained O
as O
soon O
as O
possible O
to O
prevent O

How O
Our O
Armchairs O
Are O
Made O
We O
build O

from O
a O

frame, O
using O
traditional O
methods O
and O
materials. O
With O
hand-tied O

seat, O
arms O
and O
back. O
Where O

are O
used, O
what O
makes O
them O
so O

is O
the O
high O
down O
content O
(50% O
down, O
50% O
feather O
in O
seat, O
and O
70% O
down, O
30% O
feather O
in O
back). O
The O
down O
gives O
the O
cushions O
lovely O
softness, O
while O
the O
feathers O
provide O
loft O
and O
spring.​ O
Where O
castors O
are O
used, O
they O
have O
been O
individually O

traditional O
English O

crafters O
to O
a O
very O
high O
standard, O
and O
a O
variety O
of O
finishes O
can O
be O
achieved. O
We O
use O

antique O
brass O
finish O
as O
standard. O
Where O

are O
used, O

can O

We O
use O

oak O
as O

All O

FAQs O
What O
does O
'Made-to-Order' O
mean? O
Made-to-order O
means O
that O
once O
we O
receive O
your O
order, O
it O
gets O
included O
in O
a O
production O
run O
of O
that O
item O
and O
when O
it O
is O
completed, O
it O
ships O
to O
you O
directly. O
This O
reduces O
waste O
(we O
don’t O
overproduce O
inventory O
or O
cut O
into O
materials O
that O
aren’t O
needed), O
and O
keeps O
our O
small, O
hardworking O
team O
organized. O
We O
have O
a O
limited O
number O
of O
people O
on O
our O
team O
and O
a O
made-to-order O
workflow, O
so O
we O
are O
only O
able O
to O
produce O
a O
certain O
number O
of O
items O
each O
week O
in O
order O
to O
maintain O
our O
lead O
times. O
Can O
you O
rush O
my O
order? O
We O
are O
unable O
to O
rush O
any O
made-to-order O
items, O
however O
from O
time O
to O
time O
we O

of O

lamp O
available O
on O

MENU O
Teak, O
crafts O
and O
innovationHomeProductsMaterialsteakTeakTeak O
is O
a O
close O
grained O
hardwood O
with O
a O
high O
natural O
oil O
content. O
This O
makes O
it O
hard O
wearing, O
highly O
resistant O
to O
rotting O
and O
almost O
impervious O
to O
the O
effects O
of O
sun, O
rain, O
frost O
or O
snow. O
These O
characteristics O
combine O
to O
make O
it O
the O
ideal O
timber O
for O
all O
outdoor O
applications. O
Only O
premium O
grade O
plantation-grown O
teak O
is O
used O
for O
the O
manufacture O
of O
Gloster O
furniture. O
The O
features O
of O
premium O
grade O
teak O
are O
a O
straight O
grain O
structure, O
the O
absence O
of O
knots, O
splits O
or O
cracks O
and O
an O
even O
overall O
colour.INDOOR O
USEGloster O
buffed O
teak O
benefits O
from O
an O
enhanced O
surface O
preparation O
procedure, O
where O
the O
natural O
oils O
already O
contained O
within O
the O
teak O
are O
brought O
to O
the O
surface O
and O
burnished O
to O
produce O
a O
rich O
sheen O
and O
a O
consistent O
colour. O
If O
you O
intend O
to O
use O
your O
furniture O
indoors O
or O
under O
cover O
outside O
(where O
it O
will O
not O
get O
wet), O
the O
teak O
will O
retain O
much O
of O
its O
original O
colour O
and O
the O
soft O
sheen O
of O
its O
buffed O
finish. O
Any O
marks, O
stains O
or O
damage O
to O
the O
buffed O
teak O
finish O
can O
be O
restored O
using O
the O
Gloster O
Buffed O
Teak O
Repair O
Kit.OUTDOOR O
USEGloster O
buffed O
teak O
benefits O
from O
an O
enhanced O
surface O
preparation O
procedure, O
where O
the O
natural O
oils O
already O
contained O
within O
the O
teak O
are O
brought O
to O
the O
surface O
and O
burnished O
to O
produce O
a O
rich O
sheen O
and O
a O
consistent O
colour.As O
with O
natural O
finish O
teak, O
left O
to O
age O
naturally O
outside, O
buffed O
teak O
will O
gradually O
change O
to O
a O
soft, O
silver-grey O
as O
the O
pigments O
in O
the O
surface O
layer O
of O
the O
wood O
begin O
to O
fade O
away. O
After O
the O
first O
few O
exposures O
to O
water, O
you O
should O
also O
expect O
the O
surface O
grain O
to O
rise O
slightly. O
As O
a O
part O
of O
the O
buffing O
process, O
the O
surface O
is O
wetted O
before O
final O
sanding O
to O
raise O
the O
grain, O
so O
there O
will O
be O
significantly O
less O
raised O
grain O
on O
buffed O
teak O
than O
on O
natural O
finish O
teak. O
We O
recommend O
that O
you O
allow O
your O
teak O
furniture O
to O
weather O
naturally O
this O
way O
and O
simply O
clean O
thoroughly O
once O
or O
twice O
a O
year O
with O
our O
Teak O
Cleaner. O
Buffed O
teak O
furniture O
may O
also O
benefit O
from O
an O
occasional O
light O
sanding O
to O
remove O
any O
raised O
grain O
and O
restore O
a O
smooth O
finish O
to O
the O
surface. O
Under O
no O
circumstances O
should O
a O
power O
washer O
be O
used O
to O
clean O
teak O
furniture O
as O
this O
will O
erode O
the O
surface.Because O
teak O
is O
a O
naturally O
oily O
wood, O
it O
is O
not O
possible O
to O
paint O
or O
varnish. O
Any O
paint O
or O
varnish O
applied O
will O
not O
adhere O
properly O
to O
the O
surface O
and O
after O
a O
short O
while O
will O
start O
to O
peel O
off.If O
you O
wish O
to O
retain O
the O
golden-brown O
colour O
of O
new O
teak O
we O
also O
offer O
a O
Teak O
Sealer. O
Application O
of O
Teak O
Sealer O
will O
not O
affect O
the O
strength O
or O
longevity O
of O
the O
furniture O
in O
any O
way, O
just O
its O
appearance. O
If O
you O
elect O
to O
use O
Teak O
Sealer O
you O
will O
be O
embarking O
on O
a O
regular O
maintenance O
programme O
as O
Teak O
Sealer O
needs O
to O
be O
regularly O
re-applied O
to O
provide O
continuous O
protection.If O
you O
intend O
to O
store O
your O
furniture O
over O
the O
winter, O
we O
recommend O
that O
you O
do O
so O
in O
a O
water-tight O
garden O
shed O
or O
garage. O
However, O
we O
advise O
that O
you O
do O
not O
move O
teak O
furniture O
from O
the O
garden O
straight O
into O
a O
heated O
indoor O
room O
for O
storage, O
as O
the O
sharp O
differences O
in O
temperature O
and O
humidity O
may O
cause O
the O
wood O
to O
split.To O
protect O
teak O
surfaces O
from O
staining O
and O
to O
help O
maintain O
the O
silver-grey O
patina O
on O
weathered O
teak, O
we O
recommend O
using O
our O
Teak O
Protector. O
Our O
Teak O
Protector O
creates O
an O
almost O
invisible O
shield O
which O
helps O
to O
prevent O
food O
(coffee, O
ketchup, O
red O
wine, O
olive O
oil, O
etc.) O
penetrating O
into O
the O
teak O
and O
causing O
unsightly O
stains. O
Teak O
Protector O
also O
helps O
protects O
the O
wood O
against O
the O
ingress O
of O
moisture, O
the O
adhesion O
of O
dirt O
and O
prevents O
mildew O
growth.Collections O

SOHO B-PRODUCT
HOOK I-PRODUCT
is O

The O

The O

The O

Giving O
